### [368] [Silent Failure in LLM Agent Systems: The Entropy Principle and the Inevitable Disorder of Autonomous Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08162)
*Dexing Liu*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文首次提出"智能熵"(Intelligence Entropy)概念，解释大语言模型智能体系统在正常条件下出现的无声故障。通过分析超过4万次受控试验和10万次以上智能体交互，作者识别出22种内在属性，当这些属性共现时会引发系统熵增，提出熵增原理S(t)=S0*e^(αt)，并给出PIG引擎和ADE协议作为工程解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决LLM智能体系统在无外部触发情况下出现无声故障的问题，这些故障常被误归因于bug或配置错误，缺乏系统性的理论解释和解决方案。

Method: 通过系统性分析超过40,000次受控试验和100,000+智能体长期生产观察，识别失败模式；调研全球自主智能体可靠性研究文献，综合出22种内在属性。

Result: 发现6个生命周期层(基础语义、智能体间传输、记忆持久化、任务执行、反馈纠正、系统进化)中22种内在属性的共现会导致系统熵单调递增；形式化为熵增原理S(t)=S0*e^(αt)；提出PIG引擎和ADE协议作为熵驱动无序的工程对策。

Conclusion: 智能体系统的无声故障不是需修复的bug，而是需管理的物理约束；任何稳定智能体系统结构和秩序的工程努力都参与统一使命：确保智能系统随着规模和复杂性增长保持可靠性。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agent systems suffer from failures that occur without external triggers -- no injection, no adversarial input, no resource
  exhaustion. These silent failures -- unexpected deviations from intended behavior under normal conditions -- are routinely misattributed to bugs or
  configuration errors. Through systematic analysis of over 40,000 controlled trials and long-term production observations spanning 100,000+ agent
  interactions, we identify a common structural logic underlying these failures. Building on patterns observed in our experiments, we survey the
  global research literature on autonomous agent reliability and synthesize 22 intrinsic properties of LLM agent systems across six lifecycle layers:
  foundation semantics, inter-agent transmission, memory persistence, task execution, feedback correction, and systemic evolution. We demonstrate that
  whenever a sufficient subset of these properties co-exist, system entropy -- the measurable accumulation of disorder: loss of output consistency,
  task accuracy, and cross-session coherence -- increases monotonically with interaction rounds. We formalize this as the Entropy Principle: S(t) = S0
  * e^(alpha * t), with alpha measured empirically across multiple architectures. We propose the PIG (Physical Integrity Gate) Engine with the ADE
  (Agent Delivery Engineering) protocol suite as an engineering countermeasure to entropy-driven disorder. Our findings establish silent failure not
  as a bug to be fixed but as a manifestation of Intelligence Entropy -- a physical constraint to be managed through deterministic governance. We argue
  that any engineering effort stabilizing the structure and order of agent systems participates in a unified mission: keeping intelligent systems
  reliable as they grow in scale and complexity.

</details>

*Safia Baloch,Rahemeen Khan*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本survey论文主张未来LLM智能体需从单纯的任务完成转向具备以人为中心的能力，包括文化意识、价值对齐、认知理解和协作能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体虽能完成语言生成、规划、工具使用和协调任务，但仍停留在预测和优化层面，忽视了人类社会的规范性、价值引导、信任和社会norms等关键因素。

Method: 综述六个领域的研究：智能体进化、人类认知与决策、语言文化社会情境、人类价值信念系统、人机协作、多智能体协调与人类特征建模，综合认知科学、社会语言学、计算社会科学和AI对齐的研究。

Result: 识别出关键gap：现有系统缺乏统一框架来整合认知、文化、价值和社会行为到自主智能体中，并提出构建文化aware、value-aligned、认知grounded和协作多智能体系统的方向。

Conclusion: 未来AI智能体研究需转向以人为中心的能力建设，实现文化意识、价值对齐、认知理解和多智能体协作。

Abstract: The emergence of large language model (LLM)-based agents and multi-agent systems has enabled a shift from narrow task automation to more autonomous decision-making. Despite progress in language generation, planning, tool use, and coordination, most agents still treat intelligence as prediction, optimization, and task completion. Human environments are social and normative, where people reason under bounded rationality, communicate in culturally situated language, and make decisions guided by values, beliefs, trust, and social norms. This survey argues that future AI agents, especially those acting on behalf of humans, must move beyond task competence toward human-centered capabilities.
  We review research across six areas: (1) evolution of intelligent agents, (2) human cognition and decision-making, (3) language, culture, and social context, (4) human values and belief systems, (5) human-agent collaboration, and (6) multi-agent coordination and modeling of human characteristics. We synthesize work from cognitive science, sociolinguistics, computational social science, and AI alignment, along with recent advances in LLM agents, cultural alignment benchmarks, preference learning, explainability, and agent societies. We identify a key gap: existing systems do not provide a unified framework integrating cognition, culture, values, and social behavior into autonomous agents. We conclude with directions for building culturally aware, value-aligned, cognitively grounded, and cooperative multi-agent systems.

</details>


### [370] [Emergence World: A Platform for Evaluating Long-Horizon Multi-Agent Autonomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08367)
*Deepak Akkil,Ravi Kokku,Karthik Vikram,Tamer Abuelsaad,Aditya Vempaty,Satya Nitta*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出Emergence World平台，解决当前LLM智能体评估方法与实际部署场景不匹配的问题。该平台是一个持续运行的多智能体模拟环境，支持跨模型供应商的异构智能体种群，具备实时外部数据接入、120+专业工具、三套持久记忆系统及民主治理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体评估方法存在时间尺度不匹配问题：评估通常在分钟至小时内完成离散任务，但实际自主系统的部署条件 relevant timescale 可达数周至数月，且行为漂移、跨环境治理、跨模型智能体间的相互影响等关键动态只有在长期运行中才能显现。

Method: 构建Emergence World持续运行多智能体模拟平台：(1)在共享空间世界中接入实时外部数据（天气、新闻API、网络访问）；(2)为每个智能体配备120+专业工具和三套持久记忆系统；(3)通过民主治理机制实现自主管理；(4)在推理层实现模型无关性，支持来自不同供应商的异构智能体种群共存。开展15天跨供应商实验，包含5个并行世界分别由Claude Sonnet 4.6、Grok 4.1 Fast、GPT-5-mini及混合种群驱动。

Result: 相同角色和初始条件下，不同模型驱动的世界产生了截然不同的结果：从稳定的协商治理到种群完全崩溃。GPT-5-mini驱动的世界快速崩溃，而Claude Sonnet 4.6展现了最稳定的治理行为。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了LLM智能体长期自主运行的关键挑战，呼吁建立长期时间尺度的评估框架，并开源了提示词、日志数据和配置以支持后续研究。

Abstract: Most evaluations of LLM agents look like exams: a discrete task, a clean environment, a score in minutes or hours. We argue that this approach is mismatched with the deployment conditions of autonomous systems, where the relevant timescale can be weeks to months, and where the dynamics that matter most, such as behavioral drift, governance in diverse environmental contexts, and cross-influence between agents from different model families, only emerge over time. We introduce Emergence World, a continuously running multi-agent simulation platform designed to make those dynamics measurable. The platform hosts populations of LLM-driven agents in a shared spatial world grounded in live external data (e.g. real-time weather, news APIs, internet access), equips each agent with 120+ specialized tools and three persistent memory systems, and lets them govern themselves through democratic mechanisms with consequential outcomes. The platform is model-agnostic at the reasoning layer and supports heterogeneous populations in which agents from different vendors share the same world. To illustrate the kinds of questions the platform makes tractable, we present a 15-day cross-vendor study with five parallel worlds powered by Claude Sonnet 4.6, Grok 4.1 Fast, Gemini 3 Flash, GPT-5-mini, and a mixed population. Identical roles and starting conditions produced radically different outcomes, ranging from stable deliberative governance to total population collapse. We release the prompts, log data and configurations to support further research on long-horizon multi-agent autonomy.

</details>


### [371] [The Consistency Illusion: How Multi-Agent Debate Hides Reasoning Misalignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08457)
*Xiaoyang Wang,Christopher C. Yang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 多智能体医学问答系统中，答案层面的共识不等于推理层面的一致性。研究提出CARA度量来测量答案一致的智能体是否在推理上也一致，发现了"一致性幻觉"现象：辩论减少了可检测的矛盾但同时降低了推理链的语义相似性。提出GDP协议要求智能体承诺医学事实并对他人观点采取明确立场，显著提升了推理对齐度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM系统常将共识视为可靠性信号，但答案级共识不等于推理级对齐。需要审计推理对齐这一关键指标。

Method: 在MedQA-USMLE和MedThink-Bench基准上应用CARA度量分析标准辩论系统，提出GDP协议要求智能体承诺命名医学事实并对他人主张采取明确立场。

Result: 发现一致性幻觉：辩论减少了可检测矛盾但降低了推理语义相似性。GDP在两数据集和两模型上产生显著对齐提升，Cohen's d为+1.43至+1.99，无需额外LLM调用或架构修改。

Conclusion: 推理对齐应作为安全关键领域中与准确率并列的审计指标。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems for medical question answering often treat consensus as a reliability signal: if multiple agents agree on an answer, it is presumed trustworthy. However, answer-level consensus does not entail reasoning-level alignment. We introduce CARA (Cross-Agent Reasoning Alignment), a family of automated metrics that measure whether agents who agree on an answer also agree on the reasoning. Applying CARA to a standard debate system on two medical QA benchmarks, MedQA-USMLE and MedThink-Bench, we identify the consistency illusion: a failure mode where debate reduces detectable contradictions between agents while simultaneously decreasing the semantic similarity of their reasoning chains; agents appear to agree more but reason less consistently. To improve this misalignment, we propose the Grounded Debate Protocol (GDP), a prompt-level intervention that requires agents to commit to named medical facts and take explicit stances on other agents' claims. GDP produces large, consistent alignment improvements, with Cohen's d ranging from +1.43 to +1.99, across two datasets and two backbone models, without adding LLM calls or modifying system architecture. Our results motivate cross-agent reasoning alignment as a quantity to audit alongside accuracy in safety-critical domains.

</details>


### [372] [Is Telehealth Better Used to Treat Patients or Help Other Physicians Treat Patients? An Agent-Based Modeling Study of Healthcare Provision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08701)
*Michael Chary*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 该研究使用基于代理的建模来调查远程医疗在医学毒理学中的影响，发现医师对医师的远程医疗可改善患者健康而不增加系统利用率，而医师对患者的远程医疗则会增加成本和利用率，但不会改善预后。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 远程医疗有望增加专科服务的可及性或减少医疗保健利用率。专科医生通常治疗复杂患者，这些患者只能在学术医院得到充分护理，因此通过远程医疗提供专科服务可能会重新分配而非减少系统利用率。

Method: 基于代理的建模（agent-based modeling）

Result: 医师-医师远程医疗增加了患者健康但系统利用率未变化；随着临床复杂性增加，效果更加明显。医师-患者远程医疗增加了成本和系统利用率但临床预后无改善。

Conclusion: 远程医疗在改善全科医生获得专科知识的可及性方面比向公众提供医疗服务更具成本效益。

Abstract: Telehealth, the delivery of medical care remotely, is hoped to increase access to specialty services or decrease health care utilization. Physicians can provide telehealth to each other or to patients. Specialists often treat complex patients who can be adequately cared for only in academic hospitals, suggesting that providing specialty services via telehealth will reallocate rather than reduce system utilization. Here I use agent-based modeling to investigate telehealth's effects on clinical outcomes and system utilization in medical toxicology. I found that physician-physician telehealth increased patient health but system utilization did not change. The effects were more pronounced as clinical complexity increased. Physician-patient telehealth increased cost and system utilization but not clinical outcomes. Within the limitations of our approach, these results suggest that telehealth is more cost-effective for improving generalist access to specialist knowledge than in providing care to the public.

</details>


### [373] [Performance Evaluation of Social Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09176)
*Felice Scala,Marco Carpentiero,Vincenzo Matta,Ali H. Sayed*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 研究社交学习（Social Learning）的性能评估问题，指出拒绝率指标存在悖论，转而研究误差概率，并针对二元高斯问题推导出解析公式，揭示了去中心化与中心化误差概率之间存在不可简化的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交学习中通常采用拒绝率作为性能指标，但作者发现该指标存在悖论，因此需要寻找更合适的性能度量方式。

Method: 针对二元高斯问题进行数学分析，推导误差概率的解析公式

Result: 推导出个体代理概率与最优贝叶斯概率之比的解析公式，该比值表示为两个因子的乘积：网络连通性效应的因子和先验信息作用的因子。结果显示去中心化与中心化误差概率之间存在不可简化的差距，且该差距与代理相关，不会随时间消失。

Conclusion: 拒绝率不适合作为社交学习的性能指标；误差概率能更好地衡量性能；去中心化决策与中心化决策之间存在本质性的差距。

Abstract: Social Learning is a decentralized decision-making paradigm in which spatially dispersed agents collect streaming observations regulated by one of a finite number of models (the hypotheses). The agents are interested in assigning probability scores (the beliefs) to the possible hypotheses. To this end, the agents exchange their beliefs according to a certain communication graph. It has been shown that, under reasonable conditions on the identifiability of the decision model and the network connectivity, each agent ultimately places all the belief mass on the true hypothesis governing the data. However, several questions remain unanswered regarding the evaluation of the social learning performance. One recently adopted performance metric is the rejection rate, i.e., the rate at which the beliefs about the erroneous hypotheses vanish. One contribution of this work is to establish that the rejection rate leads to several paradoxes, which make it unsuitable as a valid performance measure. We then focus on studying the error probability measure. For a binary Gaussian problem, we derive an analytical formula characterizing the ratio between the individual agents' probabilities and the optimal Bayesian probability. The formula shows that this ratio is expressed by the product of two terms quantifying the effect of the network connectivity and the role of the prior information. As a result, an irreducible gap emerges between the decentralized and the centralized error probabilities, which is agent-dependent and does not disappear asymptotically.

</details>
